# Chinese Independent Developer Projects
A curated list of projects by Chinese independent developers.

### Sub-editions
- [Programmer Edition](./pages/README-Programmer-Edition.md): For tools that require command line or coding
- [Game Edition](./pages/README-Game.md): Games only
- [2018 ~ 2020 Project List](./pages/README-2018-2020.md): Archived separately due to GitHub rendering limits

Note: You are viewing the main edition. The products listed here are ready-to-use, which differs from the product types in the sub-editions.

**1. Why this list exists**
As developers, we are curious about what side projects others are working on (whether for profit, fun, or experimentation).
So we created this repository. Developers are welcome to add their own projects~ Just submit a Pull Request or Issue <br/>
(Criteria: Must be a website or app, not developer tools or forum-style websites)

**A good one-liner matters**: ❌ `AI video generation tool` → ✅ `No editing experience needed, generate vertical short videos in 3 steps`<br/>
👉 [How to write a good one-line product description](./CONTRIBUTING-EN.md)

**2. 3 Project statuses**

| Under Development | Launched | Discontinued or Unmaintained |
|--------|--------|--------|
| :clock8: | :white_check_mark: | :x: |

## 3. Project List

## List of Chinese Independent Developer Projects
Aggregating all projects from Chinese independent developers

### Sub-forums
- [Programmer Edition](./pages/README-Programmer-Edition.md)：Requires command line or coding
- [Game Edition](./pages/README-Game.md)：All games
- [2018 ~ 2020 Project List](./pages/README-2018-2020.md)：Archived separately due to GitHub rendering limits

Note: You are currently viewing the main forum. The products listed here are ready-to-use and differ from the product types in the sub-forums.

**1. Why does this list exist**
As developers, we're naturally curious about what side projects others are working on (regardless of whether the goal is profitability, fun, or just experimenting)
That's why this repo was created. Developers are welcome to add their own projects~ Just submit a Pull Request or Issue <br/>
（Selection criteria: Must be a website or app, not a developer tool or forum-style website）

**A good introduction matters**：❌ `AI video generation tool` → ✅ `No editing experience needed, generate vertical short videos in 3 steps`<br/>
👉 [How to write a good one-line product introduction](./CONTRIBUTING.md)

**2. Projects have 3 statuses**

| In Development | Live | Closed or Unmaintained |
|--------|--------|--------|
| :clock8: | :white_check_mark: | :x: |

* :white_check_mark: [SiteCheck](https://sitecheck.top)：SiteCheck is a macOS desktop app inspired by https://ipcheck.ing, official site is sitecheck.top; I've been a loyal user of ipcheck.ing, and whenever I switch proxies, troubleshoot connections, or check DNS exit points, my first instinct is to open it. Having used it for so long, I gradually got the idea to build a similar lightweight tool myself. SiteCheck is built on that foundation — a lighter local app that lives in the macOS menubar, pulling out the tasks I use most often: checking connectivity, running DNS tests, and quickly checking my current public IP. It's not meant to replace ipcheck.ing, but to turn the parts I personally click open repeatedly every day into a more direct tool. Also, hats off to 阿禅 for giving us such a great tool.

## Recommended websites for independent developers:

### English
* [Indie Hacker](https://www.indiehackers.com/)
* [Failory](https://www.failory.com/) - Sharing stories of startup failures
* [Starter Story](https://www.starterstory.com/) - Interviews with profitable e-commerce stories, similar to Indie Hacker but focused on the e-commerce field
* [Awesome Indie](https://github.com/mezod/awesome-indie)
* [MicroConf Videos](http://www.microconf.com/starter/past-videos/)
* [Stripe Atlas Guide](https://stripe.com/atlas/guides)
* [Opps Daily - This one has a great newsletter, highly recommended to subscribe](https://www.oppslist.com/)
* [Master of Scale](https://mastersofscale.com)
* [NomadList](https://nomadlist.com/) - When working remotely, use NomadList to pick which city to go to
